            self.this.append(this)
        except __builtin__.Exception:
            self.this = this

class SourceSurfaceBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Builder of a Surface Source 

      With a surface source, you can model the light emission of a source taking into account its physical properties as the flux, the spectrum, the exitance and the intensity. A surface source can be defined with any face in a geometry which emits rays.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceSurfaceBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceSurfaceBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceSurfaceBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetFluxUnitType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetFluxUnitType(self)

    def __SetFluxUnitType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetFluxUnitType(self, value)

    def __GetFlux(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetFlux(self)

        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetFlux(self, value)
